posted:Posted April 30, 2024
msg:This is the first time I have reviewed Ctrip in so many years. The reason was that we accidentally damaged a Haier induction cooker and a Samsung TV during our stay. We notified the hotel in time the next day and explained that they would be responsible for the relevant losses. We checked the country's legal provisions and found that the actual value of compensation for damages should be based on the current market price. At the beginning, we hoped that both parties could resolve the problem in a friendly manner. If the hotel uses the market price of similar brands as the basis for payment, it would be acceptable. Unexpectedly, the hotel front desk took out a suspicious purchase order and asked us to compensate at 2-3 times the market price, and told us that if we have any doubts, please verify the purchase amount of the goods with the hotel supplier yourself. After fruitless negotiations with the front desk, we proposed to communicate with the hotel lobby manager. As a result, the manager's attitude became even worse, and he shamelessly declared that the hotel's compensation quotation was like this. We said that the price was too high and unacceptable, but the other party said that there was no room for negotiation. If you don't accept it, you can go to 12345 to complain. In the helpless situation, we can only be forced to pay a huge amount of compensation. As a five-star hotel, the attitude and overall quality of the management staff are really too poor! We also complained to Shanghai 12345 afterwards, but there has been no solution so far. The relevant authorities said that there are currently no relevant policies to regulate similar things. Once again, we advise everyone to be careful when booking hotels. It is best to find chain group hotels for five-star accommodation! 

I would like to thank Ctrip for supporting consumers. When I informed them of this incident, Ctrip customer service was very active in helping me fight for my rights. I will continue to support Ctrip as always!
